The leader’s tactical skills face challenges that will frequently question morality and the basic foundations of what we consider organized society. While city and society management will consume most of the ruler’s time, at some point exploration of the outside world is necessary to understand its history and present state.\r\n\r\nWhat decisions will you make to ensure the survival of your society?
